-# VaultLister 3.0 ΓÇö Architecture Reference
-> Generated by claude-project-scaffolder on 2026-03-02. Update when architecture changes.
-
-## System Overview
-VaultLister 3.0 is a zero-cost, offline-capable multi-channel reselling platform built on Bun.js with a vanilla JS SPA frontend and PostgreSQL database. It enables active resellers to manage inventory, cross-list to 9+ marketplaces, and automate reseller workflows with Claude AI-powered tools.
-
-## Stack
-
-| Layer | Technology | Notes |
-|-------|-----------|-------|
-| Runtime | Bun.js 1.3+ | Server + CLI scripts; faster than Node.js |
-| HTTP Server | Bun native HTTP | No Express dependency ΓÇö built-in server |
-| WebSocket | Bun native WS | Real-time listing status and automation progress |
-| Frontend | Vanilla JS SPA | Route-based chunk loading; no framework overhead |
-| Database | PostgreSQL | WAL mode + TSVECTOR full-text search; postgres |
-| Auth | JWT + bcryptjs | 15-min access / 7-day refresh; TOTP MFA |
-| Marketplace OAuth | OAuth 2.0 | eBay, Etsy, Shopify; AES-256-CBC encrypted in PostgreSQL |
-| Automations | Playwright | Headless browser bots (Poshmark, Mercari) |
-| AI | @anthropic-ai/sdk | Claude ΓÇö listing gen, image analysis, price suggestions |
-| Email | nodemailer | Gmail / Outlook OAuth for transactional email |
-| Image Storage | AWS S3 / OneDrive | Via rclone; local-first fallback |
-| Chrome Extension | Manifest V3 | Cross-listing from browser |
-| Deploy | Docker + Nginx | Multi-stage Bun 1.3 image; GitHub Actions CI/CD |
-
-## Directory Structure
-
-```
-vaultlister-3/
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ src/
-Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ backend/
-Γöé   Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ routes/          # API endpoints (inventory, listings, sales, offers, automations, AI)
-Γöé   Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ middleware/       # Auth, CSRF, rate limiting, security headers, error handling
-Γöé   Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ services/        # Business logic (email, encryption, webhook processing)
-Γöé   Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ db/              # PostgreSQL schema, migrations, seed data
-Γöé   Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ workers/         # Background jobs (sync, cleanup, price refresh)
-Γöé   Γöé   ΓööΓöÇΓöÇ server.js        # Bun HTTP server entry point
-Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ frontend/
-Γöé   Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ app.js           # Main SPA ΓÇö router, state store, API client
-Γöé   Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ index.html       # Entry point
-Γöé   Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ pages/           # Lazy-loaded route pages
-Γöé   Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ handlers/        # Event handlers grouped by domain
-Γöé   Γöé   Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ components/      # Reusable UI components
-Γöé   Γöé   ΓööΓöÇΓöÇ styles/          # CSS (nano CSS)
-Γöé   ΓööΓöÇΓöÇ shared/
-Γöé       Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ ai/              # Anthropic SDK wrappers (listing generator, price predictor, image analyzer)
-Γöé       Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ automations/     # Playwright bots (Poshmark share, follow-back, offer rules)
-Γöé       ΓööΓöÇΓöÇ utils/           # Shared utilities (escapeHtml, blockchain, AR preview, i18n)
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ tests/                   # Unit tests (Bun:test)
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ e2e/                     # Playwright E2E tests (fixtures, helpers, specs)
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ scripts/                 # Automation/utility scripts (session-start, session-end, etc.)
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ data/                    # PostgreSQL database + automation-audit.log
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ public/                  # Static assets (manifest, service worker, offline.html)
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ chrome-extension/        # Manifest V3 extension
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ mobile/                  # React Native scaffolding (V2 roadmap)
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ memory/                  # Project memory (MEMORY.md, STATUS.md)
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ docs/                    # Developer documentation
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ .claude/                 # Claude Code configuration
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ docker-compose.yml       # Web + Redis + Nginx stack
-Γö£ΓöÇΓöÇ Dockerfile               # Multi-stage Bun 1.3 image
-ΓööΓöÇΓöÇ .env.example             # Required environment variables
-```
-
-## Key Architectural Decisions
-
-### ADR-001: Bun.js Runtime
-- **Decision:** Bun.js (not Node.js) as the primary runtime
-- **Rationale:** Faster startup (<100ms cold), built-in WebSocket/HTTP server, native PostgreSQL bindings, npm ecosystem compatible
-- **Trade-off:** Smaller community; some npm packages have Bun compatibility issues; `server.close` not available (use `.stop()`)
-
-### ADR-002: Vanilla JS SPA (No Framework)
-- **Decision:** No React/Vue/Svelte ΓÇö pure vanilla JS with route-based chunk loading
-- **Rationale:** Zero framework overhead, full bundle control, no hydration complexity, offline-capable
-- **Trade-off:** More boilerplate for component patterns; harder to onboard new developers unfamiliar with vanilla JS at scale
-
-### ADR-003: PostgreSQL over PostgreSQL
-- **Decision:** PostgreSQL with WAL mode and TSVECTOR for full-text search
-- **Rationale:** Local-first architecture, zero infrastructure cost, TSVECTOR for inventory search, WAL mode for concurrent reads
-- **Trade-off:** Single writer at a time; not suitable for multi-server deployments
-
-### ADR-004: Playwright for Marketplace Automations
-- **Decision:** Playwright headless browser bots for Poshmark, Mercari, and other marketplace actions
-- **Rationale:** Official marketplace APIs are limited or inaccessible; Playwright interacts with web UIs directly
-- **Trade-off:** Bots are fragile to UI changes; platform ToS risk; must rate-limit aggressively; CAPTCHA is a blocker
-
-### ADR-005: Claude (@anthropic-ai/sdk) for AI Features
-- **Decision:** claude-haiku-4-5 for fast/cheap tasks; claude-sonnet-4-6 for listing generation and Vault Buddy
-- **Rationale:** Best multimodal capability for image-to-listing; Vault Buddy conversational help; price suggestions
-- **Trade-off:** API cost per listing; requires ANTHROPIC_API_KEY; degrade gracefully if key not set
-
-## Required Environment Variables
-
-| Variable | Required | Purpose |
-|----------|---------|---------|
-| `NODE_ENV` | Yes | Environment (development/production) |
-| `PORT` | Yes | Server port (default: 3000) |
-| `JWT_SECRET` | Yes | JWT signing secret (32+ bytes) |
-| `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` | Yes | Claude AI features (listing gen, Vault Buddy) |
-| `DB_PATH` | Yes | PostgreSQL database file path |
-| `DATA_DIR` | Yes | Data directory for DB + audit log |
-| `GITHUB_TOKEN` | Optional | GitHub MCP server |
-| `EBAY_CLIENT_ID` / `EBAY_CLIENT_SECRET` | Optional | eBay OAuth cross-listing |
-| `ETSY_API_KEY` | Optional | Etsy cross-listing |
-| Poshmark / Mercari credentials | Optional | Automation bots |
-| `AWS_*` or `RCLONE_*` | Optional | Image bank storage |
-| `SMTP_*` | Optional | Transactional email |
-
-## Authentication Flow
-
-1. User registers/logs in ΓåÆ bcryptjs (12 rounds) password hash
-2. Server issues JWT access token (15 min) + refresh token (7 days)
-3. Frontend stores via `store.persist()` (localStorage/sessionStorage)
-4. Requests include `Authorization: Bearer [token]` via `api.request()`
-5. On 401: `api.refreshAccessToken()` using stored refresh token
-6. TOTP MFA: otplib + QR code enrollment; backup codes issued at enrollment
-7. Marketplace OAuth: tokens encrypted AES-256-CBC before PostgreSQL storage
-
-## Deployment Architecture
-
-```
-Internet
-    Γöé
-[Cloudflare / DNS]
-    Γöé
-[Nginx] (SSL termination + static file serving)
-    Γöé
-[Bun.js server] :3000 (HTTP + WebSocket)
-    Γöé
-[PostgreSQL] (WAL mode, data/ volume)
-    Γöé
-[Redis] (optional ΓÇö sessions + rate limit state in production)
-```
-
-## GitHub Repository
-- Remote: https://github.com/Vaultifacts/VaultLister-3.0.git
-- Branch strategy: `main` (protected) + `feature/*`, `fix/*`, `chore/*` branches
-- CI/CD: GitHub Actions (SHA-pinned dependencies, blocking test gate)
-- Installer: Docker image via GitHub Container Registry
